  Drupal.behaviors.searchFacetModifications = {
    attach: function(context) {
      var $body = $('body');

      // If we're not on the search page do nothing.
      if(!$body.hasClass('page-search-mises')) {
        return false;
      }

      const $selectBoxes = $('#block-views-exp-mises-search-page .form-select');
      $selectBoxes.selectBox({
        mobile: true,
        menuSpeed: 'fast'
      });

      var $facetBlocks = $body.find('.region-sidebar-first .block-facetapi');

      $facetBlocks.each(function() {
        var $this = $(this);

        // Hide the block if empty.
        var emptySelector = 'p:contains("No filterable options available")';
        $this.find(emptySelector).parents('.block-facetapi').hide();

        // Update "library item" to be General.
        $this.find('#facetapi-facet-search-apimises-nodes-block-type li').each(function() {
          var $this = $(this);
          var html = $this.html();
          html = html.replace(/Library Item/g, Drupal.t("Library"));
          html = html.replace(/Wire/g, Drupal.t("Wire Articles"));
          html = html.replace(/Power &amp; Market/g, Drupal.t("Power &amp; Market Blog"));
          $this.html(html);
        });

        // Search for active filters, if found, expand the facet block.
        const $facetLinks = $this.find('.facetapi-facetapi-links');
        const $activeFilters = $facetLinks.children('li.active');

        if ($activeFilters.length) {
          $this.find('.facet-acc-trigger--closed').removeClass('facet-acc-trigger--closed');
          $this.find('.facet-acc-content--closed').removeClass('facet-acc-content--closed');
        }
      });

      // Enable facet block accordions.
      const $triggers = $('.facet-acc-trigger');
      $triggers.on('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const $this = $(this);
        const $triggerContent = $this.siblings('.facet-acc-content');
        $this.toggleClass('facet-acc-trigger--closed');
        $triggerContent.toggleClass('facet-acc-trigger--closed').slideToggle();
      });

      // Default open state for specific facets.
      $('.facet-acc-trigger--medium.facet-acc-trigger--closed').click();


      const $searchPagination = $('.view-mises-search > .text-center > .pagination');
      const $prevButton = $searchPagination.find('.prev > a');
      const $nextButton = $searchPagination.find('.next > a');

      if ($prevButton.length) {
        const $prevButtonContent = $prevButton.html() + Drupal.t('Prev');
        $prevButton.html($prevButtonContent);
      }

      if ($nextButton.length) {
        const $nextButtonContent = $nextButton.html() + Drupal.t('Next');
        $nextButton.html($nextButtonContent);
      }
    }
  };

})(jQuery, Drupal);



//this closure reserves the $.
(function ($) {
  $.fn.extend({
    equalHeight: function (options) {
      //set default height to 0 or auto
      var defaults = {
          height:null,
          minHeight: 0,
          maxHeight: null
      };
      //merge options
      options = $.extend(defaults, options);
      //cache the children (is this the parent or a group of elements)
      var children = (this.length > 1) ? this : this.children();
      if(options.height !== null){
          //if specific height is set
          children.height(options.height);
      }else{
          //set the height to auto which releases the boxes heights
          children.css('height', 'auto');
          //loop though the elements and get their heights
          children.each(function () {
              //if bigger than the default set to default
              if ($(this).height() > options.minHeight) options.minHeight= $(this).height();
              //if maxheight is set
              if(options.maxHeight !== null){
                  if(options.minHeight > options.maxHeight) options.minHeight= options.maxHeight;
              }
          });
          //set the height on all the children
          children.height(options.minHeight);
      }
      //return this so the jQuery chain is preserved
      return this;
    }
   });
})(jQuery);


(function ($) {
  Drupal.behaviors.misesColorboxDownload = {
    attach: function (context, settings) {
      if ($('#cboxLoadedContent img').length > 0) {
        $('#cboxContent .download-button').remove();
        var imageUrl = $('#cboxLoadedContent img').attr('src').split("?")[0];
        if ($('#cboxContent .download-button').length < 1) {
          $('#cboxContent').append('<div class="download-button" style="text-align: center">' +
            '<a class="button" download="' + imageUrl + '" href="' + imageUrl + '" title="Download file">Download File</a>' +
            '</div>');
          $('#cboxContent').addClass('has-download-button');
        }
      }
    }
  };

  $(document).ready(function(){
    $('body').addClass('doc-ready');
    if ("splashify" in Drupal.settings) {
      if (Drupal.settings.splashify.js_splash_active) {
        $('body').addClass('splashify-active');
      }
    }
  });

  $(window).load(function(){
    if ("splashify" in Drupal.settings) {
      if (Drupal.settings.splashify.js_splash_active) {
        $('body').addClass('splashify-active-visible');
        var checkSplashify = setInterval(function() {
          var splashifyWidth = $(".cboxIframe").contents().find(".media-splashify img").width();
          var splashifyHeight = $(".cboxIframe").contents().find(".media-splashify img").height();
          if (splashifyWidth != null && splashifyHeight != null) {
            $(".colorbox").colorbox.resize({
              innerWidth: splashifyWidth + 28,
              innerHeight: splashifyHeight + 18
            });
            clearInterval(checkSplashify);
          }
        }, 10);
      }
    }
  });

  Drupal.behaviors.disqusComments = {
    attach: function (context, settings) {
      var $powerMarketContent = $('.node-blog.view-mode-full, .node-library-item.view-mode-full');

      $powerMarketContent.once('readcomments-click').on('click', '.read-comments a', function (event) {
        // Stop click.
        event.preventDefault();
        if ($(this).parent().siblings('#disqus_thread').length > 0) {
          $('#disqus_thread').remove();
          $(this).parent().siblings('.comment-policy').hide();
          $(this).text('Load Comments');
        } else {
          $('#disqus_thread').remove();
          $('.group-right .comment-policy').hide();
          $(this).parent().siblings('.comment-policy').show();
          $(this).parents('.view-mode-full').append('<div id="disqus_thread"></div>');
          var disqus_shortname = $(this).attr('data-domain'),
            disqus_identifier = $(this).attr('data-identifier'),
            disqus_title = $(this).attr('data-url'),
            disqus_config = function () {
              this.language = 'en';
            };

          if (window.DISQUS) {

            // if Disqus exists, call it's reset method with new parameters
            DISQUS.reset({
              reload: true,
              config: function () {
                this.page.identifier = disqus_identifier;
                this.page.url = disqus_title;
                this.language = 'en';
              }
            });
          } else {
            // append the Disqus embed script to HTML
            (function () {
              var dsq = document.createElement('script');
              dsq.type = 'text/javascript';
              dsq.async = true;
              dsq.src = 'http://' + disqus_shortname + '.disqus.com/embed.js';
              (document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(dsq);
            })();
          }
          $(this).text('Hide Comments');
        }

      });

    }
  };

})(jQuery);
  </script>

  <script defer="defer">
   (function($, Drupal){
  /**
   * Move hero to main column on mobile
   */
  Drupal.behaviors.homepageHero = {
    attach: function(context, settings) {
      // show homepage hero overlay, only if
      // not empty, go over each slide
      heroBlock = $('#views_slideshow_cycle2_main_homepage_hero-block_1');
      heroBlock.find('.overlay').each(function () {
        if ($.trim($(this).html()).length) {
          $(this).show();
        }
      });

      moveHeroBlock();
      $(window).resize(function () {
        moveHeroBlock();
      });

      function moveHeroBlock() {
        var heroBlock = $('#block-views-homepage-hero-block');
        var parentElement = heroBlock.parent();
        var screen_sm_min = 768;

        if (screen.width >= screen_sm_min) {
          if (!parentElement.hasClass('region-sidebar-second-top')) {
            heroBlock.css('margin-bottom', '1em');
            heroBlock.prependTo('.region-sidebar-second-top');
            blockLocation = 'side';
          }
        }
        else {
          if (parentElement.hasClass('region-sidebar-second-top')) {
            heroBlock.css('margin-bottom', '1em');
            heroBlock.prependTo('.main-container .container .row > section');
            blockLocation = 'main';
          }
        }

      }
    }
  };

})(jQuery, Drupal);
  </script>

  <script>
   function advagg_mod_4() {
  // Count how many times this function is called.
  advagg_mod_4.count = ++advagg_mod_4.count || 1;
  try {
    if (advagg_mod_4.count <= 40) {
      var eu_cookie_compliance_cookie_name = "";

      // Set this to 100 so that this function only runs once.
      advagg_mod_4.count = 100;
    }
  }
  catch(e) {
    if (advagg_mod_4.count >= 40) {
      // Throw the exception if this still fails after running 40 times.
      throw e;
    }
    else {
      // Try again in 250 ms.
      window.setTimeout(advagg_mod_4, 250);
    }
  }
}
function advagg_mod_4_check() {
  if (window.jQuery && window.Drupal && window.Drupal.settings) {
    advagg_mod_4();
  }
  else {
    window.setTimeout(advagg_mod_4_check, 250);
  }
}
advagg_mod_4_check();
